    Feb 5, 2018 04:41 PM UTC 
    I have been trying to reproduce the problem with dynamic slots, but still no luck. I think we have two choices:

1) Back out the placement of those tmp directories from the HTCondor job slot directory back to /tmp/.

2) Ignore the few leftover directories in the execute directory. They are basically 0 size, so even though they are annoying, they do not affect anything else.

My preference is 2, but let me know what you think.

Thanks,
Mats

Eduardo

#!/bin/sh --noprofile
#chmod +x $1

#add wn-client setup
#obsolete now rpms#source /sharesoft/osg/wn/setup.sh
#add scramv1/cmssw
if [ ! $OSG_APP ]
then
/bin/sh --login
#first set OSG_APP because cmsset need it
OSG_APP="/sharesoft/osg/app"
#--- export variables -----
export OSG_APP
source /sharesoft/osg/app/cmssoft/cms/cmsset_default.sh
fi

##ed Feb22,2013#
export OSG_WN_TMP=$_CONDOR_SCRATCH_DIR
##ed Mar06,2014#
export LCG_GFAL_INFOSYS=lcg-bdii.cern.ch:2170
export LANG=C
exec "$@"

On Tue, Jan 16, 2018 at 9:25 AM, Open Science Grid FootPrints <
osg@....> wrote:

> [Duplicate message snipped]
    Jan 16, 2018 01:25 PM UTC by Sarah Schmiechen 
    Hello,

Has this change solved the problem?

Thanks,
Sarah
    Jan 10, 2018 04:41 PM UTC 
    The export OSG_WN_TMP=/tmp is happening inside the container, and /tmp in there is mapped to the scratch dir under the HTCondor directory which is the one which is not cleaned up correctly. I have not been able to reproduce the issue here, but I still think the problem is this one particular user which does a fork() between his control code and the actual computation. I have put a rule in place making sure no more of his jobs are running on your site. The rule will only show up in new glideins, so you can either wait a few days for it to automatically show up, or kill all the running and idle OSG VO jobs to have them replaced with the new version. If the leftover directory issues goes away with this change, we know it is this workload causing the problem.

I will also keep trying reproduce the problem here.

Thank you for your patience!
/Mats

by /DC=org/DC=opensciencegrid/O=Open Science Grid/OU=People/CN=Mats Rynge 45
    Jan 10, 2018 04:29 PM UTC by juaneduardo.ramirez@.... 
    Hi,
this may be a shoot in the dark.
I seeing a running pilot and inside
/var/lib/condor/execute/dir_2920383/glide_Uwo2BB/tmp/
it creates a lot of dirs like this singularity-work.xxxxxxx
However, the uncleaned ones only show one dir.
Which may indicate first, last or some special tmp is the one failing to be
deleted.

Looking at the
/var/lib/condor/execute/dir_2920383/glide_Uwo2BB/condor_job_wrapper.sh
from the pilot line 221.

I would suggest to replace
export OSG_WN_TMP=/tmp
by
export OSG_WN_TMP=$_CONDOR_SCRATCH_DIR

perhaps this that may fix the missed clean up.

Regards
Eduardo

    Well my worker nodes have a condor job wrapper in which is defined this
##ed Feb22,2013#
export OSG_WN_TMP=$_CONDOR_SCRATCH_DIR

I ended up doing this 4 years ago, because I did not know how to do if on
my ce configuration.
I know that in my ce (/etc/osg/config.d/10-storage.ini) I defined
worker_node_temp = /tmp
which gave me the original value of OSG_WN_TMP=/tmp
bacause this I use of the wrapper. This part was mosly solved long ago.

I guess the pilots still create dirs /tmp/glide_osg_xxxxxx (or
/tmp/glide_uscms3183_xxxxxx) mosly harmless,
but with singularity, I am seing also dirs like this
/tmp/.singularity-session-5458.27.2264
